         <div class="post_body"> 
          <p class="posted_info desc lighter ipsType_small"> Posted <abbr class="published" itemprop="commentTime" title="2007-05-28T12:41:48+00:00">28 May 2007 - 12:41 PM</abbr> </p> 
          <div itemprop="commentText" class="post entry-content ">
            Hi.... noob here.. so plz just bear the pain with me.. 
           <img src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAABAAAAAQCAMAAAAoLQ9TAAABxVBMVEUAAAD////343b45Hj665n776f776n888D23Wj33mv23mr332323m734G/34HL343j45YH554b777j78L3z01Tz1FX01Fb01ln011v011z12F7011/12WD12mP12mT12mb122734Hj345L45pb777rwyDzwyUDwykDxy0PwykTxy0XxzEfyzUjyzkvyz07oxkvz0VHz0VPz0lPqzFf02HH23Xz234r86af86qv76q/87LL6vAD5uwD5vADtvCntvSztvyztvy/uwjLuwTPuwTTuwzTvxTjuwTnwxzzvxTvvxjv6zT/vxUDWsT3wyEjwyFDVtEfyzlXy0nD72nX723v02Hv85Zr235r34Z7346L65qb3uQD2uAD1tgD1twD0tQDysgDwsADisiTisibQoyjSpyvyz2j31XX21n743pT23pn3357236H13qD44qPsqwDopgDkoQDdnAC7kSuwiSrxwD+yjTDuvkXvy3Xyz3v23Jfz2pv0253ingDfmwDdmQDblwDTkgC9hAG4iBytfxutgiDv0pLx1pfYkgDXkQDTjADSigDIhQCsexasfBfowXXrx37KhACvcgHeqki1jlS1j1f///9+YoenAAAAl3RSTlP///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////8A8Z+YEwAAAMdJREFUGNNjmIYGGCCUTXRMLJKAdbCFsEpUeiJMwDuMTYBHXkEpsxQiYGvOws8pJyliaJJdABKwCWFl5p4qJTZFWzO0shAoEG0lyMshI26go+7ml1MLFIhjZ+KSlTDS1fBycgmvAwrEC/GVBYjqaamm9Dpm1QMFEiwVjUt8tdVS+5LcazqAAokZytL6xa0tzcl2aRO6QNbm55kaani4Otj7t3dDHFZeZRbo6ewT1DYZ5vSiitzIiOr+iQjPNTU2dPZMQvYtAgAAVuVo53IdFCgAAAAASUVORK5CYII=" class="bbc_emoticon" alt=":)">
           <br> 
           <br> I did a logo in CorelDraw 12... The finished logo was ok.. but now the management wants to change the logo design... the fonts are the same as they were before... but now the management wants the text to be around the logo. The problem is that I had changed the text into a curve before i sent the originals for the printing.. Now i dont have the originals because they were not done on the PC that i usually use and the guy over there has formated the PC... So to cut a long story short... plz advise me and help on how to change the text back to text which is now a curve.. 
           <img src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAABAAAAAQCAMAAAAoLQ9TAAABxVBMVEUAAAD////343b45Hj665n776f776n888D23Wj33mv23mr332323m734G/34HL343j45YH554b777j78L3z01Tz1FX01Fb01ln011v011z12F7011/12WD12mP12mT12mb122734Hj345L45pb777rwyDzwyUDwykDxy0PwykTxy0XxzEfyzUjyzkvyz07oxkvz0VHz0VPz0lPqzFf02HH23Xz234r86af86qv76q/87LL6vAD5uwD5vADtvCntvSztvyztvy/uwjLuwTPuwTTuwzTvxTjuwTnwxzzvxTvvxjv6zT/vxUDWsT3wyEjwyFDVtEfyzlXy0nD72nX723v02Hv85Zr235r34Z7346L65qb3uQD2uAD1tgD1twD0tQDysgDwsADisiTisibQoyjSpyvyz2j31XX21n743pT23pn3357236H13qD44qPsqwDopgDkoQDdnAC7kSuwiSrxwD+yjTDuvkXvy3Xyz3v23Jfz2pv0253ingDfmwDdmQDblwDTkgC9hAG4iBytfxutgiDv0pLx1pfYkgDXkQDTjADSigDIhQCsexasfBfowXXrx37KhACvcgHeqki1jlS1j1f///9+YoenAAAAl3RSTlP///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////8A8Z+YEwAAAMdJREFUGNNjmIYGGCCUTXRMLJKAdbCFsEpUeiJMwDuMTYBHXkEpsxQiYGvOws8pJyliaJJdABKwCWFl5p4qJTZFWzO0shAoEG0lyMshI26go+7ml1MLFIhjZ+KSlTDS1fBycgmvAwrEC/GVBYjqaamm9Dpm1QMFEiwVjUt8tdVS+5LcazqAAokZytL6xa0tzcl2aRO6QNbm55kaani4Otj7t3dDHFZeZRbo6ewT1DYZ5vSiitzIiOr+iQjPNTU2dPZMQvYtAgAAVuVo53IdFCgAAAAASUVORK5CYII=" class="bbc_emoticon" alt=":)"> Also plz keep in mind that I do not have the font anymore with me so i recreated (traced) the font as it was on the visiting card...
           <br> 
           <br> A fast reply will be greatly appreciated...
           <br> 
           <br> Regards...
           <br> 
           <br> DJ

         <div class="post_body"> 
          <p class="posted_info desc lighter ipsType_small"> Posted <abbr class="published" itemprop="commentTime" title="2008-09-05T20:48:36+00:00">05 September 2008 - 08:48 PM</abbr> </p> 
          <div itemprop="commentText" class="post entry-content ">
            Hiii...
           <br> I won't talk about "How to Revert pre Saved Font&gt;Vector in Corel 12", I just want to leave some advise for everyone just in case they're using any "unordinary" font in corel draw.
           <br> 
           <br> Dont just uses a normal save, but use the "Prepare for Service Bureau" this will also save the font you use and can create the PDF file for previewing.
           <br> 
           <br> This is how to do it:
           <br> 1. Finish Your Design
           <br> 2. Click Menu File--&gt;Prepare for Service Bureau
           <br> 3. Choose Gather all Files associated with this document then click next
           <br> 4.Check Create a PDF file if you want to have a PDF for previewing (Color Calibration Required for best result) or just click next
           <br> 5. Browse to the destination folder 
           <br> 6. Wait for a minute until the progress is completed
           <br> 7. Then It's Done!!!
           <br> 
           <br> How to use it:
           <br> When you use another computer who doesnt have those fonts inststalled, a warning will pops up and tells you about the missing font and using a font replacement, to avoid this you can add it with Bit Stream Font Navigator This is how to add a font:
           <br> 1. Open Bit Stream Font Navigator from Corel Draw Graphic Suite
           <br> 2. Check the folder where you save the job (e.g. Removable:\Logo) then click Next 
           <br> 3. Click next and wait for searching
           <br> 4. Drag and Drop the font from Font Catalog to The Installed Font
           <br> 
           <br> If your Client want to see your design in corel you know how to open it, for quick preview I think the PDF will be easier for the client, and when the client want to print it, the service bureau will know what to do with the folder you gave (Believe me!) 
           <br> 
          </div>

            the whay i do it: make the logo keeping the font as a font, select all the logo, move a copy ( right clik ) and transform it there in curves - this way, if i want to change something, i just go to the editable text and change it there, place it in the right place ( copy ) and than transform it in curves...again and again

         <div class="post_body"> 
          <p class="posted_info desc lighter ipsType_small"> Posted <abbr class="published" itemprop="commentTime" title="2009-07-08T21:46:37+00:00">08 July 2009 - 09:46 PM</abbr> </p> 
          <div itemprop="commentText" class="post entry-content ">
            In each client's folder, I have 3 types of .cdr files. Let's say the client is "Monaco"
           <br> I will have: 
           <br> Monaco.cdr---&gt;working file where I gather my info and start ideas
           <br> Monaco_final.cdr---&gt;the final file chosen by client, not converted to curves
           <br> Monaco_final_Q.cdr---&gt;Q comes from the Ctrl. Q command that transforms to curves. This will be the file that can be opened by client or others even if they don't have my fonts. 
           <br> 
           <br> In case of any need for changing text, I always go back to my final but not converted file, and that is Monaco_final.cdr 
           <br> 
          </div>

            you can also back up your files by doing this step.
           <br> 
           <br> Go to File ---&gt; Collect for output -----&gt; Then check the (include .cdr in the 2nd option) all your files will be saved in a separate folder including pdf files and the fonts you used in that specific document. 
           <br> 
           <br> Hope this one helps.

        <div class="post_wrap"> 
         <h3 class="row2"> <span class="post_id right ipsType_small desc blend_links"> <a itemprop="replyToUrl" data-entry-pid="139012" href="https://www.designcontest.com/forum/vector-graphics/7348-how-convert-curves-back-text-coreldraw.html#entry139012" rel="bookmark" title="How to convert Curves back to Text in CorelDraw?: post #16"> #16 <img src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAABQAAAAUBAMAAAB/pwA+AAAAGFBMVEX///87QEM7QEM7QEM7QEM7QEM7QEM7QEM8ckNgAAAAB3RSTlMAEDBgj7/vdTS2ZQAAAExJREFUCNdjYEAHouWBMGZ4eSmMWV5eDmUxw5lM4eVQBYzu5algbaLlYeUlAlDN5aUKcM0GDBhMJAVI2pAMQ7EC2WJk5yA7EsnpIAAA2cAbw7DTwa0AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" class="small" title="How to convert Curves back to Text in CorelDraw?: post #16"> </a> </span> <span itemprop="creator name" class="author vcard"><a hovercard-ref="member" hovercard-id="47160" data-ipb="noparse" class="_hovertrigger url fn name " href="/designer/dskwkrs/" title="View Profile"><span itemprop="name">Dskwkrs</span></a></span> </h3> 
         <div class="author_info"> 
          <div itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" class="user_details"> 
           <span class="hide" itemprop="name">Dskwkrs</span> 
           <ul class="basic_info"> 
            <p class="desc member_title">Junior Guru</p> 
            <li class="avatar"> <img itemprop="image" src="https://designcontest-com-designcontest.netdna-ssl.com/forum/uploads/profile/xphoto-thumb-47160.gif,q_r=0.pagespeed.ic.DVQSVnx0BC.png" class="ipsUserPhoto ipsUserPhoto_large"> </li> 
            <li class="group_title"> Designer </li> 
            <li class="post_count desc lighter"> 334 posts </li> 
           </ul> 
           <ul class="custom_fields"> 
           </ul> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
         <div class="post_body"> 
          <p class="posted_info desc lighter ipsType_small"> Posted <abbr class="published" itemprop="commentTime" title="2012-07-10T09:58:14+00:00">10 July 2012 - 09:58 AM</abbr> </p> 
          <div itemprop="commentText" class="post entry-content ">
            I am not sure about Corel 12 extentions and added features but if you have the warp tools/ filters like how Ai has then it is pretty easy to wrap the text into a circle.
           <br> 1) Group all the text and then use the warp tool arch or arch in the effects menu.. which ever you choose remember that one of those will make your outer points sharp and tapered while the other just keeps it straight and warps just the middle. Sorry I forget which one is which.
           <br> 
           <br> 2) Group the text and use transform tool under the effects menu in distort and tranform. Use all of the options you have there but make sure you that you have selected the corner anchor point before you start adjusting. { Corner anchor point is located on the bottom left hand sie of the transform panel. The square with the small squares on all corners and centers. } Until you are satisfied with your resullts.
           <br> 
           <br> 3) Go and crop out a portion of the font you need to find and upload that crop to myfonts.com {what's the font}.
           <br> 
           <br> Good Luck and Happy Hunting 
           <br> 
          </div>
